Files On (PSTV)

From Vita Dev Wiki
Jump to navigation Jump to search


There are very little differences between the PS Vita and PSTV regarding file structure, but just incase anyone want's to compare, below are the file contents of a UK PSTV, with Henkaku installed along with Network Application for streaming movies and the Unit 13 demo:
